 divangat raman ke chennai nivasee bhai bies raghavan ne kaha, prakashit hui har cheez sahi he or unhone (raman ne) ise likhaa tha
 Raman died in 2013
 jab 2006 main adaalat dwaara memon kii maut kii sajaa ke bare main unhone suna tab unhone apane man kii ek naitik duvidha ke bare main likhaa tha
 Late RAW officer Raman had supported the softening of Yakub Memon, convicted in the 1993 Mumbai blasts case on the ground that he assisted the investigating agencies and was not entitled to be hanged
 tippaniyan b Raman, who retired as Additional Secretary in 1994 and was in charge of counter-terrorism, had expressed the idea by writing an article for publication, but the publication was stopped after due consideration
 lekin yah aalekh kuch din pehle prakashit hua, jisamen bataaya gaya he ki memon ko nepal se uthaaya gaya tha or baad main sibiai ne use puraani dilli railway stesan se aupchaarik rup se giraftaar kiya
 BS Raghavan, Chennai resident of late Raman said, "everything published is correct and he (raman) wrote it
" raman kaa 2013 main nidhan ho gaya tha

 kabhi-kabhi gita press ke yogadan ke bare main baat karte hue kuch log use ek dharm vishesh kii prakaashan sanstha se zyada manyata dene ko taiyaar nahin hote
 This is not appropriate
 darasal hindu dharm ke jo aarsh granth hai, ve hi bhartiya darshan or kavy ke bhi mul granth maane jate hai
 All works such as the Srimad Bhagavad Gita, Valmiki Ramayana, Mahabharata, Adhyatma Ramayana or Mahakavi Tulsi Ramcharit Manas cite examples of socio-cultural values, not only of Hinduism, but of the identity of India
 inhen jane bina bharat ko, bhartiya sahitya, kala, vigyaan ko jaananaa kathin he
 Within a short period of its inception, the Gita Press had earned a reputation as a unique contributor across the world by impeccable publication of Hindu scriptures, Indian epics and great philosophical texts and making them available to the masses at cheap prices, but Over time, he inadvertently started carrying out another Gurutara obligation
 yah tha aane vaali har peedi ko uski dharmik-saanskrithik viraasat se nirantar parichit karaate rahane kaa
 i am also a Gorakhpur resident
 is rup main bhi paaya he ki ab bhi duniya main hamaari pahchaan kaa yah sabase bada pratik chinh he
 i also had to speak with popular writers like Chetan Bhagat in a session on popular writing at the London Book Fair
 bestsellers kaa zikroor uski ek lakh prati bikne kii charchaaon ke bich jab maine kaha, main us shahar se aata hum jahaan ke ek masik kalyaan ke sthaayee graahakon kii sankhya isse do guna he to vahaan upasthit shrota samudaay ne kartal dhwani se iskaa swaagat kiya
 The Gita Press has been the most reassuring source of our reputation and recognition all over the world
 yahaan ek baat kaa zikr uchit hi hoga
 Karpatri Ji Maharaj had said about the necessary conditions for followers of Hinduism that "one who believes in the Vedas"
 anekanek granthon kaa prakaashan karne vaale gita press ne aaj tak vedon kaa prakaashan nahin kiya
 One more question is whether there is any responsibility of society and governance for the institution of such special importance? i think both have a responsibility
 agar bhartiya samaaj yah kahata he ki gita press yaa uske mukhpatr kalyaan ne unke jivan kii disha badal di he to jaahir he ki samaaj nirmaan main uski mahati bhoomika rahi he
 Now if this is the case then it also becomes the responsibility of the society to think about it

 204 India Today Group editor-in-chief Arun Purine has said that the 12 eastern states of the country contribute 16 per cent to the country's GDP along with being a major center of education and civilization
 kolkata main india today conklev east main unhone kaha ki samoochapurvi bharatvikas kiprayogshalaban chukaa he
 Read, Arun Puri's address, ladies and gentlemen, welcome to India Today Conclave East
 mujhe yahaan aakar kaaphi prasannataa ho rahi he or yahaan aae aap sabhi logon ke prati abhaari hum
 It is said that what Bengal thinks today, India thinks tomorrow
 aaj yahi baat bengal ke padosi 11 rajyon ke liye bhi kahi ja sakati he
 The entire Eastern India has become a laboratory of many competing ideas or trends in the country
 purvi bharat rachanaatmak or vidhvansak donon tarah kii bhaawanaaon kaa ek laghu swaroop he, jo bharat ko romaanchak to banaata he, saath main uljhan main bhi daalata he
 Before talking about the forces active in eastern India, i would like to give you background information in which these forces will work
 aisi ek prishthbhumi nishchit rup se agle saal hone vaala aam chunaav he
 Soon, everything will color in electoral color throughout India
 purvi bharat ke 12 rajyon main 142 loksabhaa siten hai, jo kul 543 siton kaa kareeb ek-tihaai he
 This is very important in the era of coalition politics
 pichley aam chunaavon main uttari or pashchimi rajyon main bijepi apni safalataa ke charam par rahi he, isliye is baar use in ilaakon main usase bahut zyada milane kii ummid nahin kii ja sakati
 Therefore, his emphasis will now be on eastern India
 saal 2014 main bijepi ne yahaan kii 142 siton main se 45 par jeet hasil kii thi, jinamein se 34 siten use bihar or jharkhand main mili thim
 The BJP is in government in five states of eastern India, Jharkhand, Assam, Arunachal Pradesh, Manipur and Tripura and is also the junior partner of the government in Bihar, Nagaland and Meghalaya
 iske alaava pashchim bengal, odisha, sikkim, meghalaya or nagaland main kshetreey partiyon kaa shashan he, sirf ek rajya main congress kii sarkaar he
 From this mathematics it can be understood how diverse eastern India is and how much difficulty it has to win
 har rajya kii apni alag visheshta he
 i think there are definite three types of conflicts in view of the next general election
 pehla- vikaas banaam vibhaajanvaise to yah puure bharat kii baat he, lekin khaskar yah pashchim bengal or bihar jaise rajyon main zyada praasangik he, jahaan loksabhaa kii 82 siten hai
 In Bihar, where there will be a battle of upper castes versus backward, in West Bengal between the devotees of Durga versus those who believe in Islam, then in the northeast, outer versus inner
 is conklev main aapako donon pakshon kii baat sunne ko milegi
 Politicians with competitive beliefs, as well as industrialists contributing to GDP
 doosraa- hashia banaam mukhyadharayah ek acchhee khabar he
 Slowly, but steadily, the eight states of the Northeast are moving from marginal to mainstream
 centre sarkaar sadak, railway, airport, telephone network, power project or jalmargon ke vikaas aadi ke dwaara unke ekikaran ko badhaane kii pahal kar rahi he
 For the first time an Assamese film is representing India at the Oscars and an actor of Assam origin has officially entered the Oscars on behalf of Norway
 hamane teen maheene pehle asmi ladki hima das ko world under-20 athletics championships main kamaal karte dekha he
 a Bengali girl has won the heptathlon gold medal at the recently concluded Asian Games
 is sabaki badi vajah yah he ki is kshetra main nae tazatreen netritv ubhare hai
 In the next two days you will hear four Chief Ministers of the Northeast
 teesraa- bahari or bhitari kaa takaraavaaaj jis tarah se sawaal uthaae ja rahe hai ki koun bhartiya he, koun nahin, vaisaa pehle kabhi nahin dekha gaya
 Whether it is a question of one's nationality, of geographical origin or of religion, the idea of indianness is striking
 isaki badi vajah neshnal register of citigen (NRC) bhi he
 In this way, it seems that illegal migration may become a division issue in the 2019 general election, which will have an impact on both the Trinamool Congress and the BJP in West Bengal
 to agle do dinon main garmagarm charchaa hone kii ummid he, kyonki raajnneetik diggaj pahchaan kaa sawaal uthaaenge
 But politics is not just everything in life
 is conklev main aap sangeet se lekar cinema tak jivan kii kai behatar chizon ke bare main kai pratibhavan kalakaaron kii baat sunenge
